              <h2 class="richPinName" itemprop="name">
               <a class="richPinNameLink" href="http://www.afamilyfeast.com/fresh-pineapple-peach-smoothie/" rel="nofollow">
                Fresh Pineapple Peach Smoothie
               </a>
               <meta content="https://www.pinterest.com/pin/32158584814260036/" itemprop="url"/>
               <meta content="https://s-media-cache-ak0.pinimg.com/736x/82/dc/6d/82dc6dab7b734139b860b4e51ffed83f.jpg" itemprop="image"/>
              </h2>
              <div class="richPinTitleWrapper">
               Vegetarian
                     Gluten free
                                                                                             15 mins     to make
               <span itemprop="recipeYield">
                 Makes 6 cups
               </span>
